# <a name="office-365-management-activity-api-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-103">Esquema de la API de Actividad de administración de Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-103">Office 365 Management Activity API schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-104">El esquema de la API de Actividad de administración de Office 365 se proporciona como un servicio de datos en dos niveles:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-104">The Office 365 Management Activity API schema is provided as a data service in  two layers:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-105">**Esquema común**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-105">**Common schema**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-106">La interfaz de acceso principal de Office 365 audita conceptos como el tipo de registro, la hora de creación, el tipo de usuario y la acción, y también proporciona información específica de la ubicación (como la dirección IP del cliente), las dimensiones principales (como el id. de usuario) y las propiedades específicas del producto (como el id. de objeto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-106">The interface to access core Office 365 auditing concepts such as Record Type, Creation Time, User Type, and Action as well as to provide core dimensions (such as User ID), location specifics (such as Client IP address), and product-specific properties (such as Object ID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-107">Establece vistas coherentes y uniformes para que los usuarios extraigan todos los datos de auditoría de Office 365 en varias vistas de nivel superior con los parámetros adecuados, y proporciona un esquema fijo para todos los orígenes de datos, lo que reduce significativamente el costo de aprendizaje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-107">It establishes consistent and uniform views for users to extract all Office 365 audit data in a few top level views with the appropriate parameters, and provides a fixed schema for all the data sources, which significantly reduces the cost of learning.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-108">El esquema común tiene origen en los datos del producto que pertenecen a cada equipo de producto, como Exchange, SharePoint, Azure Active Directory, Yammer y OneDrive para la Empresa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-108">Common schema is sourced from product data that is owned by each product team, such as Exchange, SharePoint, Azure Active Directory, Yammer, and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-109">Los equipos de producto pueden ampliar el campo Id. de objeto para agregar propiedades específicas del producto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-109">The Object ID field can be extended by product teams to add product specific properties.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-110">**Esquema específico del producto**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-110">**Product-specific schema**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-111">Basado en el esquema común para proporcionar un conjunto de atributos específicos del producto; por ejemplo, esquemas de Sway, esquemas de SharePoint, esquemas de OneDrive para la Empresa y esquemas de administración de Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-111">Built on top of the Common schema to provide a set of product-specific attributes; for example, Sway schema, SharePoint schema, OneDrive for Business schema, and Exchange admin schema.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-112">**¿Qué nivel debería utilizar para su escenario?**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-112">**Which layer should you use for your scenario?**</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-113">En general, si los datos están disponibles en un nivel superior, no debe volver a un nivel inferior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-113">In general, if the data is available in a higher layer, don't go back to a lower layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-114">Es decir, si se ajusta el requisito de datos en un esquema específico de producto, no es necesario volver al esquema común.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-114">In other words, if the data requirement can be fit in a product-specific schema, you don't need to go back to the Common schema.</span></span> 

## <a name="office-365-management-api-schemas"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-115">Esquemas de API de administración de Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-115">Office 365 Management API schemas</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-116">Este artículo proporciona información sobre el esquema común y sobre los esquemas específicos de cada producto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-116">This article provides details on the Common schema as well as each of the product specific schemas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-117">En la siguiente tabla se describen los esquemas disponibles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-117">The following table describes the available schemas.</span></span>

## <a name="common-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-172">Esquema común</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-172">Common schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-173">**Nombre EntityType**: AuditRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-173">**EntityType Name**: AuditRecord</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-174">Parámetro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-174">Parameter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-175">Tipo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-175">Type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-176">¿Es obligatoria?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-176">Mandatory?</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-177">Descripción</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-177">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-178">Id</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-178">Id</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-179">Combinación de GUIDEdm.Guid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-179">Combination GUIDEdm.Guid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-180">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-180">Yes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-181">Identificador único de un registro de auditoría.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-181">Unique identifier of an audit record.</span></span>|

## <a name="dlp-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1562">Esquema DLP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1562">DLP schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1563">Los eventos DLP están disponibles para Exchange Online, SharePoint Online y OneDrive para la Empresa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1563">DLP events are available for Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, and OneDrive For Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1564">Tenga en cuenta que los eventos DLP en Exchange solo están disponibles para los eventos basados en directiva DLP unificada (por ejemplo, configurados mediante el Centro de seguridad y cumplimiento).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1564">Note that DLP events in Exchange are only available for events based on unified DLP policy (e.g. configured via Security & Compliance Center).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1565">Los eventos DLP basados en las reglas de transporte de Exchange no son compatibles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1565">DLP events based on Exchange Transport Rules are not supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1566">Los eventos DLP (prevención de pérdida de datos) siempre tendrán UserKey="DlpAgent" en el esquema común.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1566">DLP (Data Loss Prevention) events will always have UserKey="DlpAgent" in the common schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1567">Hay tres tipos de DlpEvents que se almacenan como el valor de la propiedad Operation del esquema común:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1567">There are three types of DlpEvents that are stored as the value of the Operation property of the common schema:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1568">DlpRuleMatch: indica que se encontró una coincidencia con una regla.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1568">DlpRuleMatch - This indicates a rule was matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1569">Estos eventos se encuentran en Exchange, SharePoint Online y en OneDrive para la Empresa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1569">These events exist in both Exchange and SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1570">Para Exchange incluye los falsos positivos y reemplazar información.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1570">For Exchange it includes false positive and override information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1571">En SharePoint Online y en OneDrive para la Empresa, los falsos positivos y los reemplazos generan eventos independientes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1571">For SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, false positive and overrides generate separate events.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1572">DlpRuleUndo: solo existen en SharePoint Online y en OneDrive para la Empresa e indican que una acción de la directiva aplicada anteriormente se ha "deshecho", debido a la designación de falso positivo o reemplazo por el usuario, o porque el documento ya no está sujeto a directiva (ya sea debido a cambio de directiva o a cambios al contenido del documento).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1572">DlpRuleUndo - These only exist in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, and indicate a previously applied policy action has been "undone" – either because of false positive/override designation by user, or because the document is no longer subject to policy (either due to policy change or change to content in doc).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1573">DlpInfo: solo se encuentran en SharePoint Online y en OneDrive para la Empresa e indican una designación de falso positivo, pero no se ha "deshecho" ninguna acción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1573">DlpInfo - These only exist in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business and indicate a false positive designation but no action was "undone."</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1574">**Parámetros**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1574">**Parameters**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1575">**Tipo**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1575">**Type**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1576">**Obligatorio**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1576">**Mandatory**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1577">**Descripción**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1577">**Description**</span></span>|

## <a name="security-and-compliance-alerts-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1851">Esquema de alertas de seguridad y cumplimiento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1851">Security and Compliance Alerts schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1852">Las señales de alerta son:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1852">Alert signals include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1853">Todas las alertas basadas en [directivas de alerta en el centro de seguridad y cumplimiento](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/alert-policies#default-alert-policies).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1853">All alerts generated based on [Alert policies in Security & Compliance Center](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/alert-policies#default-alert-policies).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1854">Alertas relacionadas con Office 365 generadas en [Office 365 Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-cas-overview) y [Microsoft Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/cloud-app-security/what-is-cloud-app-security).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1854">Office 365 related alerts generated in [Office 365 Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-cas-overview) and [Microsoft Cloud App Security](https://docs.microsoft.com/cloud-app-security/what-is-cloud-app-security).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1855">Los UserId y UserKey de estos eventos son siempre SecurityComplianceAlerts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1855">The UserId and UserKey of these events are always SecurityComplianceAlerts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1856">Hay dos tipos de señales de alerta que se almacenan como el valor de la propiedad Operation del esquema común:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1856">There are two types of alert signals which are stored as the value of the Operation property of the common schema:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1857">AlertTriggered: una nueva alerta se genera debido a una coincidencia de directiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1857">AlertTriggered - A new alert is generated due to a policy match.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1858">AlertEntityGenerated: una nueva entidad se agrega a una alerta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1858">AlertEntityGenerated - A new entity is added to an alert.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1859">Este evento solo es aplicables a las alertas generadas en base a directivas de alerta en el Centro de seguridad y cumplimiento de Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1859">This event is only applicable to alerts generated based on Alert policies in the Office 365 Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1860">Cada alerta generada puede estar asociada con uno o varios de estos eventos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1860">Each generated alert can be associated with one or multiple of these events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1861">Por ejemplo, una directiva de alerta está definida para desencadenar una alerta si un usuario elimina más de 100 archivos en 5 minutos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1861">For example, an alert policy is defined to trigger an alert if any user deletes more than 100 files in 5 minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-1862">Si dos usuarios superan el umbral aproximadamente al mismo tiempo, habrá dos eventos AlertEntityGenerated, pero solo un evento AlertTriggered.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-1862">If two users exceed the threshold around the same time, there will be two AlertEntityGenerated events, but only one AlertTriggered event.</span></span>

## <a name="office-365-advanced-threat-protection-and-threat-investigation-and-response-schema"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2333">Esquema de Protección contra amenazas avanzada y de Investigación y respuesta de amenazas de Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2333">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Investigation and Response schema</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2334">Los eventos de [Protección contra amenazas avanzada de Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-atp) (ATP) y de Investigación y respuesta de amenazas están disponibles para los clientes de Office 365 que tienen una suscripción de Protección contra amenazas avanzada de Office 365 Plan 1, Protección contra amenazas avanzada de Office 365 Plan 2 o una suscripción de E5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2334">[Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/office-365-atp) (ATP) and Threat Investigation and Response events are available for Office 365 customers who have an Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 1, Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 2, or an E5 subscription.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2335">Cada evento en la fuente de Office 365 ATP corresponde a los siguientes que se determinaron que contienen una amenaza:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2335">Each event in the Office 365 ATP feed corresponds to the following that were determined to contain a threat:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2336">Un mensaje de correo electrónico enviado o recibido por un usuario de la organización para el que se realizan detecciones en los mensajes en el momento de entrega y de [Purga automáticamente](https://support.office.com/article/Zero-hour-auto-purge-protection-against-spam-and-malware-96deb75f-64e8-4c10-b570-84c99c674e15).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2336">An email message sent by or received by a user in the organization with detections that are made on messages at delivery time and from [Zero hour auto purge](https://support.office.com/article/Zero-hour-auto-purge-protection-against-spam-and-malware-96deb75f-64e8-4c10-b570-84c99c674e15).</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2337">Direcciones URL en las que ha hecho clic un usuario de la organización que se han detectado como malintencionadas en tiempo de clic según la protección de [Vínculos seguros de ATP de Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-safe-links).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2337">URLs clicked by a user in the organization that were detected as malicious at time-of-click based on [Office 365 ATP Safe Links](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-safe-links) protection.</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2338">Un archivo en SharePoint Online, OneDrive para la Empresa o Microsoft Teams que la protección de [Office 365 ATP](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-for-spo-odb-and-teams) ha detectado como malintencionado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2338">A file within SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Microsoft Teams that was detected as malicious by [Office 365 ATP](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/atp-for-spo-odb-and-teams) protection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2339">Una alerta que se desencadena y que inició una [investigación automatizada](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2339">An alert that is triggered and that started an [automated investigation](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2340">Las funciones de la Protección contra amenazas avanzada de Office 365 y de Investigación y respuesta de amenazas de Office 365 (anteriormente conocida como Inteligencia sobre amenazas de Office 365) ahora forman parte de la Protección contra amenazas avanzada de Office 365 Plan 2, con funciones de protección contra amenazas adicionales.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2340">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection and Office 365 Threat Investigation and Response (formerly known as Office 365 Threat Intelligence) capabilites are now part of Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 2, with additional threat protection capabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2341">Para obtener más información, consulte [Planes y precios de ATP de Office 365](https://products.office.com/exchange/advance-threat-protection) y [Descripción del servicio de ATP de Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-advanced-threat-protection-service-description).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2341">To learn more, see [Office 365 ATP plans and pricing](https://products.office.com/exchange/advance-threat-protection) and the [Office 365 ATP Service Description](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-advanced-threat-protection-service-description).</span></span>

## <a name="automated-investigation-and-response-events-in-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2668">Eventos de investigación y respuesta automatizada en Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2668">Automated investigation and response events in Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2669">Los eventos de [investigación y respuesta automatizada (AIR) de Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office) están disponibles para los clientes de Office 365 que tienen una suscripción que incluye la Protección contra amenazas avanzada de Office 365 Plan 2 u Office 365 E5.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2669">[Office 365 automated investigation and response (AIR)](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/automated-investigation-response-office) events are available for Office 365 customers who have a subscription that includes Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection Plan 2 or Office 365 E5.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2670">Los eventos de investigación se registran en función de un cambio en el estado de investigación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2670">Investigation events are logged based on a change in investigation status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2671">Por ejemplo, cuando un administrador realiza una acción que cambia el estado de una investigación de Acciones pendientes a Completada, se registra un evento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2671">For example, when an administrator takes an action that changes the status of an investigation from Pending Actions to Completed, an event is logged.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2672">Actualmente, solo se registran las investigaciones automatizadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2672">Currently, only automated investigation are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2673">(Próximamente estarán disponibles eventos para las investigaciones generadas manualmente). Se registran los siguientes valores de estado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2673">(Events for manually generated investigations are coming soon.) The following status values are logged:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2674">Investigación iniciada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2674">Investigation Started</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2676">Finalizada por el sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2676">Terminated by System</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2677">Acción pendiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2677">Pending Action</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="6bc62-2678">Amenazas encontradas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6bc62-2678">Threats Found</span></span>
